  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_94092f39-1994-4b44-8778-3b625a85f0ca'

<span id="freeTextContainer10490779935903312658">4.5 STARS!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Broken or whole… you’re all mine. You… are all mine.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>The feels. I do have a heart. Lucian Bane made we fall in love, throw my kindle, and weep like a baby. He broke my heart, then he fixed it. All in one motherfucking book. Oh, Sade. I swear I couldn't love a more complex character. He's everything I crave in one twisted package. I could read about his dark desires for 5 books, give it to me. I need it. <br/><br/><b>
  <i> The part of him that loathed his dark desires stood just behind this new </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText10490779935903312658" style="display:none">4.5 STARS!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Broken or whole… you’re all mine. You… are all mine.” </i>
</b><br /><br />The feels. I do have a heart. Lucian Bane made we fall in love, throw my kindle, and weep like a baby. He broke my heart, then he fixed it. All in one motherfucking book. Oh, Sade. I swear I couldn't love a more complex character. He's everything I crave in one twisted package. I could read about his dark desires for 5 books, give it to me. I need it. <br /><br /><b>
  <i> The part of him that loathed his dark desires stood just behind this new animal, hiding in a corner. </i>
</b><br /><br />I'm not going give you a play by play of the book, you can read it yourself. I'm going to tell you how it made me feel and why I absolutely loved it.<br /><br />I crave the darkness and in the beginning I was fed. I was so full on dark. The story had me gasping, you know, mouth wide open, like hell to the YES. Love this twistedness. The middle not so much. But here's the thing, it didn't matter because the writing had me hooked, and the characters made me laugh uncontrollably. I felt like I was fighting conflicted emotions right with Sade &amp; Mercy. Now, the end. Holy mother. I couldn't see my kindle through the tears. I kid you not. I never expected the hold this story would have on my heart until the very last bit. It's take a lot to elicit that emotion out of me. And for that, I could give a million STARS.<br /><br />Recommended as a lighter/dark read. Mild dark. Medium twisted.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1259065390" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer888345848120244010">Oh my gosh, where to start? No Mercy is incredible. My mind is still trying to process everything contained within those pages. I am left, not only breathless, but speechless. And that doesn't happen often. I am going to try to express my feelings for this book, though I can promise that there is much more than what I am able to put in this review. <br/><br/>From the first page- to the last- I kept finding that I was holding my breath. I was so caught up in the words, emotions and actions on the page, I l</span>
  <span id="freeText888345848120244010" style="display:none">Oh my gosh, where to start? No Mercy is incredible. My mind is still trying to process everything contained within those pages. I am left, not only breathless, but speechless. And that doesn't happen often. I am going to try to express my feelings for this book, though I can promise that there is much more than what I am able to put in this review. <br /><br />From the first page- to the last- I kept finding that I was holding my breath. I was so caught up in the words, emotions and actions on the page, I literally forgot to breathe. This is an intense story people. This is not a light read. This is a story that will move you to tears. <br /><br />The transformations that take place with Mercy and Sade are awe-inspiring. The struggles they face are heart-wrenching. The emotions in this book are so tangible-they jump off the pages and grip you so hard you are left dizzy. Love, fear, anguish, desire, heartache. All fall within this magnificent book.<br /> <br />I am so thankful that Lucian knows when comedic relief is needed. The placement of his humor was spot on and felt completely natural. I really needed that break. Thank you.<br /><br />The plot twists and turns will keep you guessing. Lucian is anything, but a predicable author. I found myself yelling, "Oh my god," "What the F*%&amp;," "NO WAY."<br /><br />Lucian had no mercy when writing this book. He takes the reader's emotions and puts them through the ringer and it truly is a beautiful thing. This is a first-rate author whose books and writing keep getting better with every book he writes. I am in awe of his talent. <br /><br />If I had more than 5 stars to give, I would give them gladly. This is a MUST READ series.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1267468826" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1267468826" />
    <a title="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12941902-relentlessbookchic-ramblings-reviews"><img alt="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464483219p2/12941902.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1267468826?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " class="user" itemprop="url" name="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " href="/user/show/12941902-relentlessbookchic-ramblings-reviews">RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267468826" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4370633307636058841">No Mercy picks up right where Mercy left off. Remember that feeling at the end of Mercy, where you wanted to throw your e-reader and curse the author? Yeah, well it’s back and with a vengeance. Abraham is one scary dude, I was reading those scenes with a hand over my heart and my mind going 100 miles per hour trying to figure out how in the hell they were going to get out of this nightmare. My heart broke for Mercy, Sade and Bo as they had to endure the torture at the hands of that maniac. These</span>
  <span id="freeText4370633307636058841" style="display:none">No Mercy picks up right where Mercy left off. Remember that feeling at the end of Mercy, where you wanted to throw your e-reader and curse the author? Yeah, well it’s back and with a vengeance. Abraham is one scary dude, I was reading those scenes with a hand over my heart and my mind going 100 miles per hour trying to figure out how in the hell they were going to get out of this nightmare. My heart broke for Mercy, Sade and Bo as they had to endure the torture at the hands of that maniac. These scenes are fast paced, filled with action, suspense and will emotionally drain you. <br /><br />Mercy &amp; Sade are no strangers to adversity. They have had to face it in life as well as every step of their relationship and it isn't getting any easier any time soon. In this installment it is a constant struggle against their identities and discovering newly awakened parts of themselves. Aside from all the other stuff going on in the story that will have you at the edge of your seat, Sade &amp; Mercy's push and pull is going to have you emotionally invested, exhausted and confused. It is beautiful chaos. My heart broke for Sade as he tried to reach Mercy, using everything and every part of himself he possibly could. And Mercy, OMG she broke me. I felt so many things for them throughout this book. I found myself holding my breath in many scenes, laughing in others and at some points crying. I was literally cheering for them and felt the hope disappear right along with them when they discovered something didn't work. <br /><br />The subsidiary characters were amazing in this book also. Liberty is a firecracker and she and Bo were the perfect comedic reliefs in some pretty tense situations. I would love to see Bo &amp; Liberty get their own story…Kinda need to know what happened to her hand. The book was well written with plenty of twists and turns, a unique plots and a surprise ending. Better buckle up when you read this book..it is the equivalent of being at the top of a roller coaster and throwing your hands in the air as you plummet. <br /><br />Some of my favorite quotes: <br /><br />“You are. You’re mine. You were mine whole, you’re mine broken. God, I need to fucking show you.”<br /><br />“Realized, that if I ever did remember you…I might just die because…” “I can’t love you more than I do. And I’m done trying to win your heart when it belongs to somebody else.”<br /><br />People talk about falling in love all the time, rarely do they talk about how to stay there. What I got from this book personally…it isn’t about making people remember why they fell in love with you in the first place it is about making them fall in love with you all over again, as many times as it takes. <br /><br />Relentlessbookchic approved &amp; recommended <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4370633307636058841" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Their journey is filled with tragedy and so much pain until they get rescued.<br /><br />You'll learn more about Sade &amp; Mercy and also watch love continue to form. Their story will stick with you and will touch your heart.<br /><br />Great job Lucian on another amazing read. You my friend have done it again. 'No Mercy' freaking stabbed me, twisted that knife and left me in a puddle.<br/><br/>Sade goes through so much in this book. His feelings are drastically different than the first one.   <span id="freeText887294682378665690" style="display:none">No Mercy by Lucian Bane<br />Rating: 5 stars<br /><br />'Mercy' was a stab to the heart. 'No Mercy' freaking stabbed me, twisted that knife and left me in a puddle.<br /><br />Sade goes through so much in this book. His feelings are drastically different than the first one. However, that mean dark part of him still remains. And by Gods, I love that part of him the most. His feelings for Mercy translates so much even at the turn of events.<br /><br />Abraham just....let's just say I won't have great memories on nursery rhymes for awhile.<br /><br />Bo, he was sooo sweet. You see him grow. Be proud of him.<br /><br />To those who have second thoughts of this book, DON'T. Lucian has done really well for this. I simply have no words how consuming it can be. I read it on my plane trip back home and barely felt the time pass. That's how awesome it is. One minute, and BOOM, you're stuck.</span>

  <span id="freeText5648627777776525186" style="display:none">Where to begin... I thought Mercy, the first book, was a wild ride. Lucian did not say to buckle that belt and cinch it tight, but please do when you read this book. The ride is about to get faster and bumpier. No Mercy pulls at your emotions, at your heart, and at your groin. Sade proves to be the protective hero we saw developing in book one. A new character, Liberty is introduced for more sexual tension. Fortunately, this is aimed at a recovering Bo. And then there is Mercy herself, a poor lost girl, jealous of the Mercy she no longer knows and the love that Mercy shared with Sade. Oh, Mr. Bane, you have reeled me in again and here I am waiting for book three on tenterhooks. Bring it on, soon please, Sir!</span>

  <span id="freeText16866466524771832631" style="display:none">Mentions spoilers…<br />OMG I am hooked on the Mercy series and No Mercy did not disappoint! This book leaves off right where Mercy ended and took me on a journey of every emotion under the sun from happiness, surprise, nervousness, anticipation, disgust, mortified to fanning myself during the steamy parts. I was not expecting the twist and turns that Lucian Bane took me on and felt heart broken when Mercy couldn’t remember Sade. I thought I couldn’t love Sade any more than I did in Mercy but was proven wrong in this book. Sade is everything I’m looking for in a book – he’s a big, sexy, bad ass, dirty talking, alpha with a sense of humor, broken beyond belief and when he finally finds love he loves hard and with an intensity that can melt your panties right off your body with just one look. Mercy is still a bad ass chick with a smart mouth and together they make this story AWESOME! I also love that we get to know Bo better and he totally cracks me up with all his one-liners and comments about Liberty’s mechanical hand – I mean WTF, who thinks up this shit? Oh yeah, Lucian Bane! There were parts of this story that had me laughing my ass off! I love how this book is a perfect blend of dark and twisted with the perfect amount of humor. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8154691530398828334">OH HOLY HELL!<br/><br/>My emotions, so many emotions!<br/><br/>I laughed, cried, pretty sure I screamed, was on the edge of my seat and just an full emotional wreck!<br/><br/>I can honestly say I dont think I have ever felt so many different feeling during one book before.   <span id="freeText8154691530398828334" style="display:none">OH HOLY HELL!<br /><br />My emotions, so many emotions!<br /><br />I laughed, cried, pretty sure I screamed, was on the edge of my seat and just an full emotional wreck!<br /><br />I can honestly say I dont think I have ever felt so many different feeling during one book before. Lucian Bane, truly takes you on one hell of a ride throughout this captivating book. I couldn't put it down, look away or but I would of attacked any human that dare intruded! Freaking hell I could barely breathe throughout the whole thing - in the best way!<br /><br />Sade and Mercy are thrown into one hell of a nightmare in No Mercy: A Darker Continuation. The book picks up exactly where Mercy (book 1) ended and rockets off with the first sentence. Lucian's writing pulls you into the depths of each character so that you see what they see and feel what they feel. The personal struggles and conflicts of each of the characters inspires the reader to take a good hard look in the mirror. Lucian has a message for the reader, lessons taught chapter by chapter. The sex scenes are scorching!!!!!<br /><br />Oh, Mr.Sade. I swear I couldn't love a more complex character. He's everything I crave in one twisted package.<br /><br />The compelling love between Sade and Mercy is so powerful! It's beautiful, dark, soul twisting and although there love is so strong, it is also so relatable.<br /><br />The humour throughout No Mercy is perfectly placed, Lucian knows the exact points where it is needed and it felt completely natural.<br /><br />The plot twists and turns will keep you guessing. Lucian is anything, but a predicable author. I found myself yelling and never knowing what was going to come next. It is definitely one of the reasons Lucian is such an amazing author because you may never know what your going to get but you know for damn sure it will be F*%&amp;ing awesome!<br /><br />This book will definitely have you hooked in and not let you go. I am simply addicted to Sade and Mercy's story and progressing on this journey with them. I cannot wait to read more of this story.<br /><br />Highly recommended!! If I could give more than 5 stars then I would!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8154691530398828334" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17743854396995066963">This series is an absolute MUST READ. I have to admit that I was nervous to read Book 1, because I was afraid of all the feelings and emotions this author would inevitably bring out.   <span id="freeText17743854396995066963" style="display:none">This series is an absolute MUST READ. I have to admit that I was nervous to read Book 1, because I was afraid of all the feelings and emotions this author would inevitably bring out. Lucian has a tendency to hit the proverbial nail on the head with me, and this series didn't disappoint. It's raw, it's gritty, it's highly addictive. I couldn't put down Book 1 until it was finished, and while the wait for Book 2 seemed like it took forever, once released, I devoured every word until it was done. I've never been good at writing reviews, but I can tell you that if you like the darker aspects of BDSM - a little pain with your pleasure - this series is definitely one you should check out. In fact, once you've finished reading these two books...make sure you check out the rest of Lucian's books. I promise you won't be disappointed.</span>

I'm terrified of giving something away and would not want to spoil it for anyone. <br /><br />This book is absolutely amazing It picks up right where Mercy left off and will leave you breathless. Lucian Bane writes the most hold your breath, in the edge of your seat, non stop page turning books I've ever read. You will not be disappointed in this book at all. <br /><br />Thank you Lucian for writing such amazing books. I love Slade and Mercy so much and the story of them is beyond fantastic.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3971070427519451167" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VWbNU/vyKmwbBqSwHjH62VsosolcYu9ahYnTAU1xGVrQh5GspubRDOh5Xr/EXt0sa7U4oOOwY2xb4vcZkG5Ozg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RcHEZEnvUnDY28wZl6aLVVt+J74stcvggXQ8IOrojUrAIJibFPupECukNhZNyayga+Otl5NnR9ZfHxg4N/fa3g==')})
  }
//]]>
